  Authã¯å†…éƒ¨çš„ã«ã€ŒClerkã€ã¨ã„ã†èªè¨¼ã‚µãƒ¼ãƒ“ã‚¹ã‚’åˆ©ç”¨ã—ã¦ã„ã¾ã™ã€‚å®Ÿè£…ã«ã¯ã€Neonã®ç®¡ç†ç”»é¢ï¼ˆConsoleï¼‰ã®ã€ŒAuthã€ã‚¿ãƒ–ã«è¨˜è¼‰ã•ã‚Œã¦ã„ã‚‹ä»¥ä¸‹ã®

  ã“ã‚Œã‚‰ãŒæƒãˆã°ã€ã€Œãƒ­ã‚°ã‚¤ãƒ³ãƒœã‚¿ãƒ³ã‚’æŠ¼ã™ã¨noteåˆ†æãŒå§‹ã¾ã‚‹ã€ã¨ã„ã†ã‚¹ãƒ ãƒ¼ã‚ºãªä½“é¨“ã‚’å®Ÿè£…ã§ãã¾ã™ã€‚

> Neon Authã«**Clerk Publishable/Secret Keyã‚„JWKS URLã¯ã‚ã‚Šã¾ã›ã‚“**ã€‚ãã‚Œã¯Clerkã‚µãƒ¼ãƒ“ã‚¹ã‚’ä½¿ã†å ´åˆã®ã¿ã§ã™ã€‚ Neon Authã¯Neon Data
  APIã®**API Keyã ã‘ã§å®Œçµ**ï¼ˆæ—¢ã«å–å¾—æ¸ˆã¿ï¼‰ã€‚[1][2][3]

  ## 1. Neon Auth + Streamlit æœ€çŸ­ã‚³ãƒ¼ãƒ‰

  ```python
  # app.py
  import streamlit as st
  import requests
  import os
  from dotenv import load_dotenv

  load_dotenv()

  NEON_DATA_API_URL = os.getenv("NEON_DATA_API_URL")  # https://xxxxx.data-api.neon.tech
  NEON_API_KEY = os.getenv("NEON_API_KEY")           # neon_xxxxx...

  if "token" not in st.session_state:
      st.session_state.token = None

  # === ãƒ­ã‚°ã‚¤ãƒ³ ===
  if not st.session_state.token:
      with st.form("login"):
          email = st.text_input("Email")
          password = st.form_submit_button("ãƒ­ã‚°ã‚¤ãƒ³")

          if password:
              response = requests.post(
                  f"{NEON_DATA_API_URL}/v1/rpc/sign_in",
                  headers={"Authorization": f"Bearer {NEON_API_KEY}"},
                  json={"email": email, "password": password}
              )

              if response.status_code == 200:
                  st.session_state.token = response.json()["token"]
                  st.success("ãƒ­ã‚°ã‚¤ãƒ³æˆåŠŸï¼")
                  st.rerun()
              else:
                  st.error("ãƒ­ã‚°ã‚¤ãƒ³å¤±æ•—")

  # === ãƒ­ã‚°ã‚¢ã‚¦ãƒˆ ===
  else:
      st.sidebar.success(f"ğŸ‘‹ {email}")
      if st.sidebar.button("ãƒ­ã‚°ã‚¢ã‚¦ãƒˆ"):
          st.session_state.token = None
          st.rerun()

      # === DBæ“ä½œä¾‹ï¼ˆRLSè‡ªå‹•é©ç”¨ï¼‰ ===
      st.header("ãƒ‡ãƒ¼ã‚¿è¡¨ç¤º")
      headers = {"Authorization": f"Bearer {st.session_state.token}"}

      # ãƒ†ãƒ¼ãƒ–ãƒ«ä¸€è¦§
      tables = requests.get(f"{NEON_DATA_API_URL}/v1/", headers=headers).json()
      st.write("ãƒ†ãƒ¼ãƒ–ãƒ«:", tables)

      # ãƒ¦ãƒ¼ã‚¶ãƒ¼å°‚ç”¨ãƒ‡ãƒ¼ã‚¿ï¼ˆRLSæƒ³å®šï¼‰
      if st.button("è‡ªåˆ†ã®ãƒ‡ãƒ¼ã‚¿å–å¾—"):
          data = requests.get(f"{NEON_DATA_API_URL}/users", headers=headers).json()
          st.json(data)
  ```

  **å®Ÿè¡Œ**: `pip install streamlit requests python-dotenv` â†’ `streamlit run app.py`

  ## 2. Neon Authç®¡ç†ç”»é¢ã®Redirect URIè¨­å®š

  **Neon Authã«ã¯Redirect URIè¨­å®šä¸è¦**ã§ã™ã€‚Data APIã¯REST APIç›´å©ããªã®ã§ã€OAuthãƒ•ãƒ­ãƒ¼ãªã—ã€‚[3]

  | ç’°å¢ƒ | Redirect URI | å¿…è¦ï¼Ÿ |
  |------|-------------|--------|
  | **ãƒ­ãƒ¼ã‚«ãƒ«** | ä¸è¦ï¼ˆ`http://localhost:8501`ï¼‰ | âŒä¸è¦ |
  | **Render** | ä¸è¦ï¼ˆ`https://your-app.onrender.com`ï¼‰ | âŒä¸è¦ |

  ## 3. Neonç®¡ç†ç”»é¢ã®ã‚­ãƒ¼ç¢ºèªçµæœ

  ```
  âœ… Clerk Publishable Key: ãªã—ï¼ˆClerkæœªä½¿ç”¨ï¼‰
  âœ… Clerk Secret Key: ãªã—ï¼ˆClerkæœªä½¿ç”¨ï¼‰
  ```

    1 CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION sign_in(email text, password text)
    2 RETURNS json AS $$
    3 DECLARE
    4     user_record record;
    5 BEGIN
    6     -- ãƒ¦ãƒ¼ã‚¶ãƒ¼ã®ç…§åˆ
    7     SELECT * INTO user_record FROM app_users WHERE app_users.email = sign_in.email;
    8
    9     -- ãƒ‘ã‚¹ãƒ¯ãƒ¼ãƒ‰ã®æ¤œè¨¼
   10     IF user_record.password_hash = crypt(password, user_record.password_hash) THEN
   11         RETURN json_build_object(
   12             'status', 'success',
   13             'token', encode(gen_random_bytes(32), 'hex'), -- ç°¡æ˜“çš„ãªãƒˆãƒ¼ã‚¯ãƒ³ç”Ÿæˆ
   14             'email', user_record.email
   15         );
   16     ELSE
   17         RAISE EXCEPTION 'Invalid email or password';
   18     END IF;
   19 END;
   20 $$ LANGUAGE plpgsql SECURITY DEFINER;

  main()DeltaGeneratorDeltaGenerator(_provided_cursor=LockedCursor(_index=4, _parent_path=(1, 1, 1), _props={'delta_type':
  'markdown', 'add_rows_metadata': None}), _parent=DeltaGenerator(_provided_cursor=RunningCursor(_parent_path=(1, 1, 1), _index=5),
  _parent=DeltaGenerator(_provided_cursor=RunningCursor(_parent_path=(1...
  Creator of Delta protobuf messages.

  Parameters
  ----------
  root_container: BlockPath_pb2.BlockPath.ContainerValue or None
    The root container for this DeltaGenerator. If None, this is a null
    DeltaGenerator which doesn't print to the app at all (useful for
    testing).

  cursor: cursor.Cursor or None
    This is either:
    - None: if this is the running DeltaGenerator for a top-level
      container (MAIN or SIDEBAR)
    - RunningCursor: if this is the running DeltaGenerator for a
      non-top-level container (created with dg.container())
    - LockedCursor: if this is a locked DeltaGenerator returned by some
      other DeltaGenerator method. E.g. the dg returned in dg =
      st.text("foo").

  parent: DeltaGenerator
    To support the `with dg` notation, DGs are arranged as a tree. Each DG
    remembers its own parent, and the root of the tree is the main DG.

  block_type: None or "vertical" or "horizontal" or "column" or "expandable"
    If this is a block DG, we track its type to prevent nested columns/expanders
  dgproperty    Get our DeltaGenerator.
  idproperty    Property attribute.
  add_rowsmethod    Concatenate a dataframe to the bottom of the current one.
  altair_chartmethod    Display a chart using the Vega-Altair library.
  area_chartmethod    Display an area chart.
  audiomethod    Display an audio player.
